\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_LMAX}{MMGS\_LMAX}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define MMGS\+\_\+\+LMAX~1024}

Maximum array size when storing adjacent points (or ball) of a vertex.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgs_8h_af1bc8381952d0a0961ba02fac70a9796}{MMGS\+\_\+\+Param}}}



Input parameters for mmg library.

\index{libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}!MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv@{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv}}
\index{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv@{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv}!libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv()}{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Compute\+\_\+eigenv (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{m\mbox{[}6\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{lambda\mbox{[}3\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{vp\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em m} & upper part of a symetric matric diagonalizable in $\vert$R \\
\hline
{\em lambda} & array of the metric eigenvalues \\
\hline
{\em vp} & array of the metric eigenvectors\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the order of the eigenvalues
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute the real eigenvalues and eigenvectors of a symetric matrice m whose upper part is provided (m11, m12, m13, m22, m23, m33 in this order). lambda\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}0,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(1,\+:) in fortran lambda\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}1,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}1,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(2,\+:) in fortran lambda\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}2\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}2,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}2,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(3,\+:) in fortran

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+COMPUTE\+\_\+\+EIGENV(m,lambda,vp,retval)~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: m($\ast$)~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: lambda($\ast$),vp($\ast$)~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\end{DoxyReturn}
Find the indices of the 3 adjacent elements of triangle {\itshape kel}. $v_i = 0$ if the $i^{th}$ face has no adjacent element (so we are on a boundary face).

\hline

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_nonBdyEdge()}{MMGS\_Get\_nonBdyEdge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+non\+Bdy\+Edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{idx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em e0} & pointer toward the first extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em e1} & pointer toward the second extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer toward the edge reference. \\
\hline
{\em idx} & index of the non boundary edge to get (between 1 and nb\+\_\+edges) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get extremities {\itshape e0}, {\itshape e1} and reference {\itshape ref} of the idx$^\wedge$th non boundary edge (for DG methods for example). An edge is boundary if it is located at the interface of 2 domains witch different references, if it belongs to one triangle only or if it is a singular edge (ridge or required).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: idx~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\index{libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}!MMGS\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges@{MMGS\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges}}
\index{MMGS\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges@{MMGS\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges}!libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges()}{MMGS\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+number\+Of\+Non\+Bdy\+Edges (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{nb\+\_\+edges }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em nb\+\_\+edges} & pointer toward the number of non boundary edges. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get the number of non boundary edges (for DG methods for example). An edge is boundary if it is located at the interface of 2 domains with different references, if it belongs to one triangle only or if it is a singular edge (ridge or required). Append these edges to the list of edge.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
reallocate the edge array and append the internal edges. This may modify the behaviour of other functions.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+NUMBEROFNONBDYEDGES(mesh,nb\+\_\+edges,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT)\+:: nb\+\_\+edges~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_vertices()}{MMGS\_Get\_vertices()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+vertices (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{vertices,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{refs,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{are\+Corners,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{are\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em vertices} & pointer toward the table of the points coordinates. The coordinates of the $i^{th}$ point are stored in vertices\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$3\mbox{]}@3. \\
\hline
{\em refs} & pointer to the table of the point references. The ref of the $i^th$ point is stored in refs\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em are\+Corners} & pointer toward the table of the flags saying if points are corners. are\+Corners\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}=1 if the $i^{th}$ point is corner. \\
\hline
{\em are\+Required} & pointer toward the table of flags saying if points are required. are\+Required\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}=1 if the $i^{th}$ point is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get the coordinates and references of the mesh vertices.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Init\_mesh()}{MMGS\_Init\_mesh()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int}]{starter,  }\item[{}]{... }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em starter} & dummy argument used to initialize the variadic argument list \\
\hline
{\em ...} & variadic arguments.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
For the MMGS\+\_\+mmgslib function, you need to call the {\itshape MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh} function with the following arguments \+: MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met, \&your\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the MMGS\+\_\+mmgsls function, you need to call the {\itshape MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh} function with the following arguments \+: MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls, \&your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

Here,{\itshape your\+\_\+mesh} is a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}, {\itshape your\+\_\+metric} and {\itshape your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set} are {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 if fail
\end{DoxyReturn}
MMG structures allocation and initialization.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
No fortran interface to allow variadic arguments. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+save\+Msh\+Mesh\+\_\+and\+\_\+all\+Data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}} $\ast$}]{sol,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer toward the solution structure. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of file. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Write mesh and a list of data fields (that are considered as solutions and not metrics, thus, we do nothing over the ridge points) at MSH file format (.msh extension). Save file at ASCII format for .msh extension, at binary format for .mshb one.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: strlen0~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Set\_ithSols\_inSolsAtVertices()}{MMGS\_Set\_ithSols\_inSolsAtVertices()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+ith\+Sols\+\_\+in\+Sols\+At\+Vertices (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{int}]{i,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{s }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sol} & pointer toward the array of solutions \\
\hline
{\em i} & position of the solution field that we want to set. \\
\hline
{\em s} & table of the solutions at mesh vertices. The solution at vertex {\itshape k} is given by s\mbox{[}k-\/1\mbox{]} for a scalar sol, s\mbox{[}3$\ast$(k-\/1)\mbox{]}@3 for a vectorial solution and s\mbox{[}6$\ast$(k-\/1)\mbox{]}@6 for a tensor solution.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set values of the solution at the ith field of the solution array ({\itshape i} from 1 to nb\+\_\+sols).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: i~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), DIMENSION($\ast$),INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: s~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+local\+Parameter (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{int}]{typ,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ref,  }\item[{double}]{hmin,  }\item[{double}]{hmax,  }\item[{double}]{hausd }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set local parameters\+: set the hausdorff value at {\itshape hausd}, the minmal edge size value at {\itshape hmin} and the maximal edge size value at {\itshape hmax} for all elements of type {\itshape typ} and reference {\itshape ref}.

\index{MMGS\_Set\_lsBaseReference@{MMGS\_Set\_lsBaseReference}!libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}{MMGS\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+ls\+Base\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{br }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer toward the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em br} & new level-\/set base reference. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set a new level-\/set base reference of ref {\itshape br} in ls discretization mode. Based references are boundary conditions to which implicit domain can be attached. All implicit volumes that are not attached to listed base references are deleted as spurious volumes by the {\itshape rmc} option.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+LSBASEREFERENCE(mesh,sol,br,retval)~\newline

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN)\+:: br~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}
